    TEXT[!MUST]:       freely by any implementer.

SPECIFICATION: https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9615
  SECTION: [Updates to RFCs](#section-2)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Therefore, child DNS operators and parental agents wishing to use
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    CDS/CDNSKEY records for initial DS enrollment SHOULD support the
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    authentication protocol described here.

  SECTION: [Chain of Trust](#section-3.1)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    If a child DNS operator implements this specification, each signaling
    TEXT[!MUST]:    zone MUST be signed and be validatable by the parental agent (i.e.,
    TEXT[!MUST]:    have a valid publicly resolvable DNSSEC chain of trust).

  SECTION: [Signaling Names](#section-3.2)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    To publish information about the child zone in an authenticated
    TEXT[!MUST]:    fashion, the child DNS operator MUST publish one or more signaling
    TEXT[!MUST]:    records at a signaling name under each signaling domain.
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Signaling records MUST be accompanied by RRSIG records created with
    TEXT[!MUST]:    the corresponding signaling zone's key(s).

  SECTION: [Signaling Consent to Act as the Child's Signer](#section-4.1)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    To confirm its willingness to act as the child's delegated signer and
    TEXT[!MUST]:    authenticate the child's CDS/CDNSKEY RRsets, the child DNS operator
    TEXT[!MUST]:    MUST copublish them at the corresponding signaling name under each
    TEXT[!MUST]:    signaling domain, excluding those that would fall within the child
    TEXT[!MUST]:    domain (Section 3.2).
    TEXT[!MAY]: For simplicity, the child DNS operator MAY
    TEXT[!MAY]:    also copublish the child's CDS/CDNSKEY RRsets under signaling domains
    TEXT[!MAY]:    within the child domain, although those signaling domains are not
    TEXT[!MAY]:    used for validation (Section 4.2).
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Unlike the CDS/CDNSKEY RRsets at the child's apex, a signaling RRset
    TEXT[!MUST]:    MUST be signed with the corresponding signaling zone's key(s).
    TEXT[!MUST]: Its
    TEXT[!MUST]:    contents MUST be identical to the corresponding RRset published at
    TEXT[!MUST]:    the child's apex.
    TEXT[!MUST]: To exclude the possibility of semantic collision,
    TEXT[!MUST]:    there MUST NOT be a zone cut at a signaling name.

  SECTION: [Validating CDS/CDNSKEY Records for DNSSEC Bootstrapping](#section-4.2)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    To validate a child's CDS/CDNSKEY RRset for DNSSEC bootstrapping, the
    TEXT[!MUST]:    parental agent, knowing both the child zone name and its NS
    TEXT[!MUST]:    hostnames, MUST execute the following steps:
    TEXT[!MUST]:    The parental agent MUST abort the procedure if an error condition
    TEXT[!MUST]:    occurs, in particular:

  SECTION: [Triggers](#section-4.3)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Parental agents SHOULD trigger the procedure described in Section 4.2
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    once one of the following conditions is fulfilled:
    TEXT[!MUST]: For example, when discovering signaling
    TEXT[!MUST]:    names by performing an NSEC walk or zone transfer of a signaling
    TEXT[!MUST]:    zone, the parental agent MUST NOT assume that a nameserver under
    TEXT[!MUST]:    whose signaling domain a signaling record appears is actually
    TEXT[!MUST]:    authoritative for the corresponding child.
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Instead, whenever a list of "bootstrappable domains" is obtained by
    TEXT[!MUST]:    means other than directly from the parent, the parental agent MUST
    TEXT[!MUST]:    ascertain that the delegation actually contains the nameserver
    TEXT[!MUST]:    hostname seen during discovery, and ensure that signaling-record
    TEXT[!MUST]:    queries are only made against the proper set of nameservers as listed
    TEXT[!MUST]:    in the child's delegation from the parent.

  SECTION: [Child DNS Operator](#section-5.1)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Signaling domains SHOULD be delegated as standalone zones, so that
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    the signaling zone's apex coincides with the signaling domain (such
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    as _signal.ns1.example.net).

  SECTION: [Parental Agent](#section-5.2)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]: It is thus RECOMMENDED that
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    queries into signaling domains be performed with an (initially) empty
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    resolver cache, or that some other method for retrieving fresh data
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    from authoritative servers be used.
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    It is also RECOMMENDED that QNAME minimization [RFC9156] be used when
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    resolving queries for signaling records to guard against certain
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    attacks (see Section 6).

SPECIFICATION: https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9715
  SECTION: [Introduction](#section-1)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    [RFC7766] states that all general-purpose DNS implementations MUST
    TEXT[!MUST]:    support both UDP and TCP transport.

  SECTION: [Proposed Recommendations for UDP Responders](#section-3.1)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]: UDP responders should compose response packets that fit in the
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           minimum of the offered requestor's maximum UDP payload size
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           [RFC6891], the interface MTU, the network MTU value configured
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           by the knowledge of the network operators, and the RECOMMENDED
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           maximum DNS/UDP payload size 1400.

  SECTION: [Proposed Recommendations for UDP Requestors](#section-3.2)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]: UDP requestors should limit the requestor's maximum UDP
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           payload size to fit in the minimum of the interface MTU, the
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           network MTU value configured by the network operators, and the
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:           RECOMMENDED maximum DNS/UDP payload size 1400.

  SECTION: [Weaknesses of IP Fragmentation](#section-7.3)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Section 3.2 of [RFC8085] states that "an application SHOULD NOT send
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    UDP datagrams that result in IP packets that exceed the Maximum
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Transmission Unit (MTU) along the path to the destination".

  SECTION: [Details of Requestor's Maximum UDP Payload Size Discussions](#appendix-A)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    *  [RFC4035] states that "A security-aware name server MUST support
    TEXT[!MUST]:       the EDNS0 ([RFC2671]) message size extension, [and it] MUST
    TEXT[!MUST]:       support a message size of at least 1220 octets".

SPECIFICATION: https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9904
  SECTION: [Abstract](#name-abstract)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    This document does not change the recommendation status (MUST, MAY,
    TEXT[!MUST]:    RECOMMENDED, etc.) of the algorithms listed in RFC 8624; that is the
    TEXT[!MUST]:    work of future documents.

  SECTION: [Updating Algorithm Requirement Levels](#section-1.2)
    TEXT[!MUST]: Unless there
    TEXT[!MUST]:    are strong security reasons, an algorithm is expected to be
    TEXT[!MUST]:    downgraded from MUST to NOT RECOMMENDED or MAY, instead of directly
    TEXT[!MUST]:    from MUST to MUST NOT.
    TEXT[!MUST]: Similarly, an algorithm that has not been
    TEXT[!MUST]:    mentioned as mandatory to implement is expected to be first
    TEXT[!MUST]:    introduced as RECOMMENDED instead of a MUST.
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    Since the effect of using an unknown DNSKEY algorithm is that the
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    zone is treated as insecure, it is recommended that algorithms that
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    have been downgraded to NOT RECOMMENDED or lower not be used by
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    authoritative nameservers and DNSSEC signers to create new DNSKEYs.
    TEXT[!MUST]: Once an algorithm has reached a sufficiently low level of
    TEXT[!MUST]:    deployment, it can be marked as MUST NOT, so that recursive resolvers
    TEXT[!MUST]:    can remove support for validating it.
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Validating recursive resolvers are encouraged to retain support for
    TEXT[!MUST]:    all algorithms not marked as MUST NOT.

  SECTION: [Requirements Notation](#section-1.3)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    [RFC2119] considers the term SHOULD to be equivalent to RECOMMENDED,
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    and SHOULD NOT equivalent to NOT RECOMMENDED.
    TEXT[!SHOULD]: This document has
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    chosen to use the terms RECOMMENDED and NOT RECOMMENDED, as this more
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    clearly expresses the recommendations to implementers.

  SECTION: [Adding and Changing Values](#section-2.2)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |  Adding a new entry to the "Digest Algorithms" registry with a
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |  recommended value of "MAY" in the "Use for DNSSEC Delegation",
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |  "Use for DNSSEC Validation", "Implement for DNSSEC Delegation", or
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |  "Implement for DNSSEC Validation" columns SHALL follow the
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |  Specification Required policy as defined in [RFC8126].

  SECTION: [DNS Security Algorithm Numbers Registry Column Values](#section-3)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    When there are multiple RECOMMENDED algorithms in the "Use for"
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    columns, operators should choose the best algorithm according to
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    local policy.
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +===+===============+===========+===========+===========+===========+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |No.|Mnemonics      |Use for    |Use for    |Implement  |Implement  |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |   |               |DNSSEC     |DNSSEC     |for DNSSEC |for DNSSEC |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |   |               |Signing    |Validation |Signing    |Validation |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +===+===============+===========+===========+===========+===========+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |1  |RSAMD5         |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |3  |DSA            |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+

    TEXT[!MUST]:    |   |               |RECOMMENDED|           |RECOMMENDED|           |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |6  |DSA-NSEC3-SHA1 |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |7  |RSASHA1-NSEC3- |NOT        |RECOMMENDED|NOT        |MUST       |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |   |SHA1           |RECOMMENDED|           |RECOMMENDED|           |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |8  |RSASHA256      |RECOMMENDED|RECOMMENDED|MUST       |MUST       |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |10 |RSASHA512      |NOT        |RECOMMENDED|NOT        |MUST       |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |   |               |RECOMMENDED|           |RECOMMENDED|           |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |12 |ECC-GOST       |MUST NOT   |MAY        |MUST NOT   |MAY        |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |13 |ECDSAP256SHA256|RECOMMENDED|RECOMMENDED|MUST       |MUST       |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+

    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |253|PRIVATEDNS     |MAY        |MAY        |MAY        |MAY        |

    TEXT[!MUST]:    |254|PRIVATEOID     |MAY        |MAY        |MAY        |MAY        |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +---+---------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+-----------+

  SECTION: [Digest Algorithms Registry Column Values](#section-4)
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    When there are multiple RECOMMENDED algorithms in the "Use for"
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    columns, operators should choose the best algorithm according to
    TEXT[!SHOULD]:    local policy.
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +=====+===========+===========+===========+==========+=============+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |Value|Description|Use for    |Use for    |Implement | Implement   |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |     |           |DNSSEC     |DNSSEC     |for DNSSEC| for DNSSEC  |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |     |           |Delegation |Validation |Delegation| Validation  |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +=====+===========+===========+===========+==========+=============+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |0    |NULL (CDS  |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT   |MUST NOT  | MUST NOT    |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |     |only)      |           |           |          |             |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |1    |SHA-1      |MUST NOT   |RECOMMENDED|MUST NOT  | MUST        |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |2    |SHA-256    |RECOMMENDED|RECOMMENDED|MUST      | MUST        |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |3    |GOST R     |MUST NOT   |MAY        |MUST NOT  | MAY         |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |     |34.11-94   |           |           |          |             |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |4    |SHA-384    |MAY        |RECOMMENDED|MAY       | RECOMMENDED |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |5    |GOST R     |MAY        |MAY        |MAY       | MAY         |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |     |34.11-2012 |           |           |          |             |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+
    TEXT[!MUST]:    |6    |SM3        |MAY        |MAY        |MAY       | MAY         |
    TEXT[!MUST]:    +-----+-----------+-----------+-----------+----------+-------------+

  SECTION: [Security Considerations](#section-5)
    TEXT[!MUST]: In this document, the
    TEXT[!MUST]:    algorithms identified as MUST or RECOMMENDED to implement are not
    TEXT[!MUST]:    known to be broken at the current time, and cryptographic research so
    TEXT[!MUST]:    far leads us to believe that they are likely to remain adequately
    TEXT[!MUST]:    secure unless significant and unexpected discovery is made.

  SECTION: [Operational Considerations](#section-6)
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Upgrading an algorithm at the same time as rolling to the new Key
    TEXT[!MUST]:    Signing Key (KSK) key will lead to DNSSEC validation failures, and
    TEXT[!MUST]:    users MUST upgrade the DS algorithm first before rolling to a new
    TEXT[!MUST]:    KSK.
